<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>
<s> there are savage murmurs from the crowd brown <\s>
<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>
<s> a small restless harassed man with a fighting face there's always blacklegs it's the nature of em <\s>
<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>
<s> there is a movement and old thomas joining the crowd takes his stand in front harness <\s>
<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>
<s> the unions live by justice not to one but all <\s>
<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>
<s> i don't say you go too far for that which you're entitled to but you're going too far for the moment you've dug a pit for yourselves <\s>
<s> are you to stay there or are you to climb out <\s>
<s> a clean cut welshman with a dark moustache you've hit it mister <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> another movement in the crowd and rous coming quickly takes his stand next thomas harness <\s>
<s> cut your demands to the right pattern and we ll see you through refuse and don't expect me to waste my time coming down here again <\s>
<s> i m not the sort that speaks at random as you ought to know by this time <\s>
<s> if you're the sound men i take you for no matter who advises you against it he fixes his eyes on roberts you ll make up your minds to come in and trust to us to get your terms <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> hands together and victory or the starvation you've got now <\s>
<s> a prolonged murmur from the crowd jago <\s>
<s> sullenly talk about what you know <\s>
<s> lifting his voice above the murmur know <\s>
<s> with cold passion all that you've been through my friend i ve been through i was through it when i was no bigger than pointing to a youth that shaver there the unions then were n't what they are now <\s>
<s> what's made them strong <\s>
<s> it's hands together that s made them strong <\s>
<s> i ve been through it all i tell you the brand's on my soul yet <\s>
<s> i know what you ve suffered there's nothing you can tell me that i don't know but the whole is greater than the part and you are only the part <\s>
<s> stand by us and we will stand by you <\s>
<s> quartering them with his eyes he waits <\s>
<s> the murmuring swells the men form little groups <\s>
<s> green bulgin and lewis talk together lewis <\s>
<s> speaks very sensible the union chap <\s>
<s> if i d a been listened to you'd ave eard sense these two months past <\s>
<s> the bargemen are seen laughing <\s>
<s> pointing look at those two blanks over the fence there <\s>
<s> with gloomy violence they'd best stop their cackle or i ll break their jaws <\s>
<s> suddenly you say the furnace men's paid enough <\s>
<s> i did not say they were paid enough i said they were paid as much as the furnace men in similar works elsewhere <\s>
<s> hubbub what about harper's <\s>
<s> with cold irony you may look at home for lies my man <\s>
<s> harper's shifts are longer the pay works out the same <\s>
<s> a dark edition of his brother george will ye support us in double pay overtime saturdays <\s>
<s> what have ye done with our subscriptions <\s>
<s> coldly i have told you what we will do with them <\s>
<s> will it's always will <\s>
<s> ye'd have our mates desert us <\s>
<s> shouting hold your row <\s>
<s> evans looks round angrily harness <\s>
<s> lifting his voice those who know their right hands from their lefts know that the unions are neither thieves nor traitors <\s>
<s> i ve said my say <\s>
<s> figure it out my lads when you want me you know where i shall be <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>

<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>

<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>

<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>
<s> the unions live by justice not to one but all <\s>
<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>

<s> which is it to be <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>
<s> there are savage murmurs from the crowd brown <\s>
<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>

<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>
<s> there is a movement and old thomas joining the crowd takes his stand in front harness <\s>
<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>

<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>

<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>
<s> there are savage murmurs from the crowd brown <\s>
<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>
<s> a small restless harassed man with a fighting face there's always blacklegs it's the nature of em <\s>
<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>
<s> there is a movement and old thomas joining the crowd takes his stand in front harness <\s>
<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>
<s> the unions live by justice not to one but all <\s>
<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>
<s> i don't say you go too far for that which you're entitled to but you're going too far for the moment you've dug a pit for yourselves <\s>
<s> are you to stay there or are you to climb out <\s>
<s> a clean cut welshman with a dark moustache you've hit it mister <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> another movement in the crowd and rous coming quickly takes his stand next thomas harness <\s>
<s> cut your demands to the right pattern and we ll see you through refuse and don't expect me to waste my time coming down here again <\s>
<s> i m not the sort that speaks at random as you ought to know by this time <\s>
<s> if you're the sound men i take you for no matter who advises you against it he fixes his eyes on roberts you ll make up your minds to come in and trust to us to get your terms <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> hands together and victory or the starvation you've got now <\s>
<s> a prolonged murmur from the crowd jago <\s>
<s> sullenly talk about what you know <\s>
<s> lifting his voice above the murmur know <\s>
<s> with cold passion all that you've been through my friend i ve been through i was through it when i was no bigger than pointing to a youth that shaver there the unions then were n't what they are now <\s>
<s> what's made them strong <\s>
<s> it's hands together that s made them strong <\s>
<s> i ve been through it all i tell you the brand's on my soul yet <\s>
<s> i know what you ve suffered there's nothing you can tell me that i don't know but the whole is greater than the part and you are only the part <\s>
<s> stand by us and we will stand by you <\s>
<s> quartering them with his eyes he waits <\s>
<s> the murmuring swells the men form little groups <\s>
<s> green bulgin and lewis talk together lewis <\s>
<s> speaks very sensible the union chap <\s>
<s> if i d a been listened to you'd ave eard sense these two months past <\s>
<s> the bargemen are seen laughing <\s>
<s> pointing look at those two blanks over the fence there <\s>
<s> with gloomy violence they'd best stop their cackle or i ll break their jaws <\s>
<s> suddenly you say the furnace men's paid enough <\s>
<s> i did not say they were paid enough i said they were paid as much as the furnace men in similar works elsewhere <\s>
<s> hubbub what about harper's <\s>
<s> with cold irony you may look at home for lies my man <\s>
<s> harper's shifts are longer the pay works out the same <\s>
<s> a dark edition of his brother george will ye support us in double pay overtime saturdays <\s>
<s> what have ye done with our subscriptions <\s>
<s> coldly i have told you what we will do with them <\s>
<s> will it's always will <\s>
<s> ye'd have our mates desert us <\s>
<s> shouting hold your row <\s>
<s> evans looks round angrily harness <\s>
<s> lifting his voice those who know their right hands from their lefts know that the unions are neither thieves nor traitors <\s>
<s> i ve said my say <\s>
<s> figure it out my lads when you want me you know where i shall be <\s>
<s> he jumps down the crowd gives way he passes through them and goes away <\s>
<s> a bargeman looks after him jerking his pipe with a derisive gesture <\s>
<s> the men close up in groups and many looks are cast at roberts who stands alone against the wall evans <\s>
<s> he wants ye to turn blacklegs that's what he wants <\s>
<s> he wants ye to go back on us <\s>
<s> sooner than turn blackleg i d starve i would <\s>
<s> who's talkin o blacklegs mind what you're saying will you <\s>
<s> a youth with yellow hair and huge arms what about the women <\s>
<s> they can stand what we can stand i suppose can't they <\s>
<s> an don't want one <\s>
<s> raising his voice aye <\s>
<s> give us the power to come to terms with london lads <\s>
<s> a dark slow fly gloomy man go up the platform if you got anything to say go up an say it <\s>
<s> there are cries of thomas <\s>
<s> he is pushed towards the platform he ascends it with difficulty and bares his head waiting for silence <\s>
<s> a hush red haired youth <\s>
<s> suddenly coot old thomas <\s>
<s> jan run to the lion say i sent you for mrs <\s>
<s> with a feeble movement i'll just sit quiet madge <\s>
<s> giving jan a slice of bread there ye little rascal <\s>
<s> going to the fire she kneels it's going out <\s>
<s> with a faint smile t is all the same <\s>
<s> jan begins to blow his whistle madge <\s>
<s> tsht you jan stops mrs <\s>
<s> smiling let im play madge <\s>
<s> on her knees at the fire listening waiting an waiting <\s>
<s> i've no patience with it waiting an waiting that's what a woman has to do <\s>
<s> can you hear them at it i can <\s>
<s> jan begins again to play his whistle madge gets up half tenderly she ruffles his hair then sitting leans her elbows on the table and her chin on her hands <\s>
<s> behind her on mrs <\s>
<s> roberts's face the smile has changed to horrified surprise <\s>
<s> she makes a sudden movement sitting forward pressing her hands against her breast <\s>
<s> then slowly she sinks back slowly her face loses the look of pain the smile returns <\s>
<s> she fixes her eyes again on jan and moves her lips and finger to the tune the curtain falls <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>
<s> there are savage murmurs from the crowd brown <\s>
<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>
<s> a small restless harassed man with a fighting face there's always blacklegs it's the nature of em <\s>
<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>
<s> there is a movement and old thomas joining the crowd takes his stand in front harness <\s>
<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>
<s> the unions live by justice not to one but all <\s>
<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>
<s> i don't say you go too far for that which you're entitled to but you're going too far for the moment you've dug a pit for yourselves <\s>
<s> are you to stay there or are you to climb out <\s>
<s> a clean cut welshman with a dark moustache you've hit it mister <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> another movement in the crowd and rous coming quickly takes his stand next thomas harness <\s>
<s> cut your demands to the right pattern and we ll see you through refuse and don't expect me to waste my time coming down here again <\s>
<s> i m not the sort that speaks at random as you ought to know by this time <\s>
<s> if you're the sound men i take you for no matter who advises you against it he fixes his eyes on roberts you ll make up your minds to come in and trust to us to get your terms <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> hands together and victory or the starvation you've got now <\s>

<s> it's hands together that s made them strong <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>
<s> there are savage murmurs from the crowd brown <\s>
<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>
<s> a small restless harassed man with a fighting face there's always blacklegs it's the nature of em <\s>
<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>
<s> there is a movement and old thomas joining the crowd takes his stand in front harness <\s>
<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>
<s> the unions live by justice not to one but all <\s>
<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>
<s> i don't say you go too far for that which you're entitled to but you're going too far for the moment you've dug a pit for yourselves <\s>
<s> are you to stay there or are you to climb out <\s>
<s> a clean cut welshman with a dark moustache you've hit it mister <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> another movement in the crowd and rous coming quickly takes his stand next thomas harness <\s>
<s> cut your demands to the right pattern and we ll see you through refuse and don't expect me to waste my time coming down here again <\s>
<s> i m not the sort that speaks at random as you ought to know by this time <\s>
<s> if you're the sound men i take you for no matter who advises you against it he fixes his eyes on roberts you ll make up your minds to come in and trust to us to get your terms <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> hands together and victory or the starvation you've got now <\s>

<s> sullenly talk about what you know <\s>

<s> what's made them strong <\s>
<s> it's hands together that s made them strong <\s>

<s> stand by us and we will stand by you <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>
<s> there are savage murmurs from the crowd brown <\s>
<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>
<s> a small restless harassed man with a fighting face there's always blacklegs it's the nature of em <\s>
<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>
<s> there is a movement and old thomas joining the crowd takes his stand in front harness <\s>
<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>
<s> the unions live by justice not to one but all <\s>
<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>
<s> i don't say you go too far for that which you're entitled to but you're going too far for the moment you've dug a pit for yourselves <\s>
<s> are you to stay there or are you to climb out <\s>
<s> a clean cut welshman with a dark moustache you've hit it mister <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> another movement in the crowd and rous coming quickly takes his stand next thomas harness <\s>
<s> cut your demands to the right pattern and we ll see you through refuse and don't expect me to waste my time coming down here again <\s>
<s> i m not the sort that speaks at random as you ought to know by this time <\s>
<s> if you're the sound men i take you for no matter who advises you against it he fixes his eyes on roberts you ll make up your minds to come in and trust to us to get your terms <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> hands together and victory or the starvation you've got now <\s>
<s> a prolonged murmur from the crowd jago <\s>
<s> sullenly talk about what you know <\s>
<s> lifting his voice above the murmur know <\s>
<s> with cold passion all that you've been through my friend i ve been through i was through it when i was no bigger than pointing to a youth that shaver there the unions then were n't what they are now <\s>
<s> what's made them strong <\s>
<s> it's hands together that s made them strong <\s>
<s> i ve been through it all i tell you the brand's on my soul yet <\s>
<s> i know what you ve suffered there's nothing you can tell me that i don't know but the whole is greater than the part and you are only the part <\s>
<s> stand by us and we will stand by you <\s>
<s> quartering them with his eyes he waits <\s>
<s> the murmuring swells the men form little groups <\s>
<s> green bulgin and lewis talk together lewis <\s>
<s> speaks very sensible the union chap <\s>
<s> if i d a been listened to you'd ave eard sense these two months past <\s>

<s> coldly i have told you what we will do with them <\s>
<s> will it's always will <\s>
<s> ye'd have our mates desert us <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>

<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>

<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>

<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>

<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>

<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>
<s> the unions live by justice not to one but all <\s>
<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>

<s> which is it to be <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>
<s> there are savage murmurs from the crowd brown <\s>
<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>

<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>
<s> there is a movement and old thomas joining the crowd takes his stand in front harness <\s>
<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>

<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>

<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>
<s> there are savage murmurs from the crowd brown <\s>
<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>
<s> a small restless harassed man with a fighting face there's always blacklegs it's the nature of em <\s>
<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>
<s> there is a movement and old thomas joining the crowd takes his stand in front harness <\s>
<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>
<s> the unions live by justice not to one but all <\s>
<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>
<s> i don't say you go too far for that which you're entitled to but you're going too far for the moment you've dug a pit for yourselves <\s>
<s> are you to stay there or are you to climb out <\s>
<s> a clean cut welshman with a dark moustache you've hit it mister <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> another movement in the crowd and rous coming quickly takes his stand next thomas harness <\s>
<s> cut your demands to the right pattern and we ll see you through refuse and don't expect me to waste my time coming down here again <\s>
<s> i m not the sort that speaks at random as you ought to know by this time <\s>
<s> if you're the sound men i take you for no matter who advises you against it he fixes his eyes on roberts you ll make up your minds to come in and trust to us to get your terms <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> hands together and victory or the starvation you've got now <\s>
<s> a prolonged murmur from the crowd jago <\s>
<s> sullenly talk about what you know <\s>
<s> lifting his voice above the murmur know <\s>
<s> with cold passion all that you've been through my friend i ve been through i was through it when i was no bigger than pointing to a youth that shaver there the unions then were n't what they are now <\s>
<s> what's made them strong <\s>
<s> it's hands together that s made them strong <\s>
<s> i ve been through it all i tell you the brand's on my soul yet <\s>
<s> i know what you ve suffered there's nothing you can tell me that i don't know but the whole is greater than the part and you are only the part <\s>
<s> stand by us and we will stand by you <\s>
<s> quartering them with his eyes he waits <\s>
<s> the murmuring swells the men form little groups <\s>
<s> green bulgin and lewis talk together lewis <\s>
<s> speaks very sensible the union chap <\s>
<s> if i d a been listened to you'd ave eard sense these two months past <\s>
<s> the bargemen are seen laughing <\s>
<s> pointing look at those two blanks over the fence there <\s>
<s> with gloomy violence they'd best stop their cackle or i ll break their jaws <\s>
<s> suddenly you say the furnace men's paid enough <\s>
<s> i did not say they were paid enough i said they were paid as much as the furnace men in similar works elsewhere <\s>
<s> hubbub what about harper's <\s>
<s> with cold irony you may look at home for lies my man <\s>
<s> harper's shifts are longer the pay works out the same <\s>
<s> a dark edition of his brother george will ye support us in double pay overtime saturdays <\s>
<s> what have ye done with our subscriptions <\s>
<s> coldly i have told you what we will do with them <\s>
<s> will it's always will <\s>
<s> ye'd have our mates desert us <\s>
<s> shouting hold your row <\s>
<s> evans looks round angrily harness <\s>
<s> lifting his voice those who know their right hands from their lefts know that the unions are neither thieves nor traitors <\s>
<s> i ve said my say <\s>
<s> figure it out my lads when you want me you know where i shall be <\s>
<s> he jumps down the crowd gives way he passes through them and goes away <\s>
<s> a bargeman looks after him jerking his pipe with a derisive gesture <\s>
<s> the men close up in groups and many looks are cast at roberts who stands alone against the wall evans <\s>
<s> he wants ye to turn blacklegs that's what he wants <\s>
<s> he wants ye to go back on us <\s>
<s> sooner than turn blackleg i d starve i would <\s>
<s> who's talkin o blacklegs mind what you're saying will you <\s>
<s> a youth with yellow hair and huge arms what about the women <\s>
<s> they can stand what we can stand i suppose can't they <\s>
<s> an don't want one <\s>
<s> raising his voice aye <\s>
<s> give us the power to come to terms with london lads <\s>
<s> a dark slow fly gloomy man go up the platform if you got anything to say go up an say it <\s>
<s> there are cries of thomas <\s>
<s> he is pushed towards the platform he ascends it with difficulty and bares his head waiting for silence <\s>
<s> a hush red haired youth <\s>
<s> suddenly coot old thomas <\s>
<s> jan run to the lion say i sent you for mrs <\s>
<s> with a feeble movement i'll just sit quiet madge <\s>
<s> giving jan a slice of bread there ye little rascal <\s>
<s> going to the fire she kneels it's going out <\s>
<s> with a faint smile t is all the same <\s>
<s> jan begins to blow his whistle madge <\s>
<s> tsht you jan stops mrs <\s>
<s> smiling let im play madge <\s>
<s> on her knees at the fire listening waiting an waiting <\s>
<s> i've no patience with it waiting an waiting that's what a woman has to do <\s>
<s> can you hear them at it i can <\s>
<s> jan begins again to play his whistle madge gets up half tenderly she ruffles his hair then sitting leans her elbows on the table and her chin on her hands <\s>
<s> behind her on mrs <\s>
<s> roberts's face the smile has changed to horrified surprise <\s>
<s> she makes a sudden movement sitting forward pressing her hands against her breast <\s>
<s> then slowly she sinks back slowly her face loses the look of pain the smile returns <\s>
<s> she fixes her eyes again on jan and moves her lips and finger to the tune the curtain falls <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>
<s> there are savage murmurs from the crowd brown <\s>
<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>
<s> a small restless harassed man with a fighting face there's always blacklegs it's the nature of em <\s>
<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>
<s> there is a movement and old thomas joining the crowd takes his stand in front harness <\s>
<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>
<s> the unions live by justice not to one but all <\s>
<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>
<s> i don't say you go too far for that which you're entitled to but you're going too far for the moment you've dug a pit for yourselves <\s>
<s> are you to stay there or are you to climb out <\s>
<s> a clean cut welshman with a dark moustache you've hit it mister <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> another movement in the crowd and rous coming quickly takes his stand next thomas harness <\s>
<s> cut your demands to the right pattern and we ll see you through refuse and don't expect me to waste my time coming down here again <\s>
<s> i m not the sort that speaks at random as you ought to know by this time <\s>
<s> if you're the sound men i take you for no matter who advises you against it he fixes his eyes on roberts you ll make up your minds to come in and trust to us to get your terms <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> hands together and victory or the starvation you've got now <\s>

<s> it's hands together that s made them strong <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>

<s> scene ii it is past four <\s>
<s> in a grey failing light an open muddy space is crowded with workmen <\s>
<s> beyond divided from it by a barbed wire fence is the raised towing path of a canal on which is moored a barge <\s>
<s> in the distance are marshes and snow covered hills <\s>
<s> the works high wall runs from the canal across the open space and ivy the angle of this wall is a rude platform of barrels and boards <\s>
<s> on it harness is standing <\s>
<s> roberts a little apart from the crowd leans his back against the wall <\s>
<s> on the raised towing path two bargemen lounge and smoke indifferently <\s>
<s> holding out his hand well i've spoken to you straight <\s>
<s> if i speak till to morrow i can't say more <\s>
<s> a dark sallow spanish looking man with a short thin beard mister want to ask you <\s>
<s> can they get blacklegs <\s>
<s> menacing let em try <\s>
<s> there are savage murmurs from the crowd brown <\s>
<s> a round faced man where could they get em then <\s>
<s> a small restless harassed man with a fighting face there's always blacklegs it's the nature of em <\s>
<s> there's always men that'll save their own skins <\s>
<s> there is a movement and old thomas joining the crowd takes his stand in front harness <\s>
<s> holding up his hand they can't get them <\s>
<s> but that won't help you <\s>
<s> now men be reasonable <\s>
<s> your demands would have brought on us the burden of a dozen strikes at a time when we were not prepared for them <\s>
<s> the unions live by justice not to one but all <\s>
<s> any fair man will tell you you were ill advised <\s>
<s> i don't say you go too far for that which you're entitled to but you're going too far for the moment you've dug a pit for yourselves <\s>
<s> are you to stay there or are you to climb out <\s>
<s> a clean cut welshman with a dark moustache you've hit it mister <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> another movement in the crowd and rous coming quickly takes his stand next thomas harness <\s>
<s> cut your demands to the right pattern and we ll see you through refuse and don't expect me to waste my time coming down here again <\s>
<s> i m not the sort that speaks at random as you ought to know by this time <\s>
<s> if you're the sound men i take you for no matter who advises you against it he fixes his eyes on roberts you ll make up your minds to come in and trust to us to get your terms <\s>
<s> which is it to be <\s>
<s> hands together and victory or the starvation you've got now <\s>

<s> sullenly talk about what you know <\s>

<s> what's made them strong <\s>
<s> it's hands together that s made them strong <\s>

<s> stand by us and we will stand by you <\s>
